So to newbie traders (and i assume 95% reading this thread are newbies) stick to fibs and trendlines. Yes it is difficult but very rewarding. I am glad to teach you trendlines in my own thread if many peole request it. Don't worry, there won't be any indicators for sale, just teaching you plan basic trading with trendlines. Here is my contribution to FX-50....BTW, I like the name and had an M5 system I traded for a while called x50 and I still glance at regularly.

I have the faster CCI combination...21 and 89 along with the stochastic histogram. However, I use M1 and M5 gann to help me see what is happening for entry. And I've removed all the other junk from the chart...candles and gann only as I moving more and more toward trading the price action and candle formation on M5 and M15, with M1 for entry.

H1 and H4 are crutial for me to see if I might catch a runner for a 50+ pip move or more. M1 for entry and move to higher timeframes if the scalp turns into a trend.

I use 1-2-3 and fractals on M5 and M15 and I'm drawing trendlines on those timeframes and looking for breaks.

This trade was +10.

Cheers

CanuckCT

--- 帖子 #89 ---
Have you put all the indicators in the indicator folder

If not

Save the indicators to experts/indicators and install all the indicators ending in ex4 and mq4

For the temolate install the tpl 1 min and 5 min in the templates folder of mt 4

To attach to charts, click on charts in the upper tool bar then a dropdown in the dropdown select templates and look for the fxprime template and add it to your chart

If you are still having problems pm me and I will talk you through it.

--- 帖子 #90 ---
Also, after you copy the files over to the experts/indicators folder, you have to restart MT4 before they will show up in your list of indicators.  (alternatively, you can click on Tools and then Metaquotes Language Editor and push the "Compile" button, and then you don't have to re-start MT4)

--- 帖子 #93 ---
Today is a bit tough...London session has good move but last few hours a bit tricky. For me today, using price action and glancing at FX50

EJ +29 - 4 trades

GJ +40 - 1 trade

Use M5 and M15 to view consolidation area...need to be patient for a break and need to take pips quickly.

FXPrime is a moving average crossover system and by it's nature it lags badly. Price is always ahead of moving averages....so by the time the indicators fire, you are too late because the price has reach the top or bottom of the consolidation area. This is why the original entry waits for CCI to establish and gets you into the trade with CCI34 crossing back to joing CCI170....you are trading the pullback and return to the prevailing trend.  Assuming there is a trend.  You can also see that by looking at price and a 34 and 170 moving average on a chart. Have a look...that's all CCI represents...how far price is from a moving average.

This is why you need to look for trendlines, support and resistance and higher time frames to see what is happening because that is where price turns. You can trade the turn and when it doesn't turn you can trade the break.

Sometime FXPrime helps with this...sometimes it doesn't.

For example, if the H1 candle is bearish...hits a trendline and you begin to watch it recover fully to a bullish candle, that's when you can start to identify tradeable moves....use price action or FXPrime to enter...chances are it will at least go a few pips in your favor. Move stop to breakeven after 10 pips, maybe take the 10 pips and move on.

If you blindly follow FXPrime with no other reference point....that's a bit tricky.

I suggest you go to demo mode and take a blank chart with no indicators....or use trade simulator. See if you can buy when price goes up and sell when price goes down. Sounds easy. But you'll be wrong a lot. The point of the exercise is what to do when you are wrong. That's what you need to practice. Some of the FXPrime setups really cloud price movement with the HA candles. Especially when price going sideways....so you have to practice what to do when you are wrong.

Cheers

CanuckCT

--- 帖子 #99 ---
FXPrime vs Price Action - USDCAD

With FXPrime you are waiting to catch a mini trend. I've marked a couple of trades...the first long is good for a few and the second sell works out ok.

Using price action....there are lots of lines you could draw as the day progresses and play the breaks above and below various points of support and resistance. You might have played the break of S1 and been wrong....that trade should have been closed quickly and would have been a good time to sell.

If we begin to use price a bit more...you'll be able to tell when FXPrime signal is good or not.

Cheers

CanuckCT

CanuckCT

You guys are so on my page I had to make a post.

First off props to CD, this method is so close to mine and although I'm not 100% Canadian I did grow up in Vancouver, so similarities all round.

I have combined my method and CD's and have the template below. I attach a zip with my templates, indicators and scripts for anyone to use if they like.

http://www.forexfactory.com/attachme...1&d=1227524330

Never underestimate the power of bull candle eating bear candle (or vice versa) as a confirmation to your trade and great place for your stop loss, this confirmation signal usually comes before the RSI. This pic is from this morning on the e/j, I also took a similar setup on the g/u.

Basically I have made the uselsss areas of RSI grey so we do ont see them and use the 13 period. My cci is 144 and 34 period. The magenta line is a triple stoch as close to the M15 stoch I could get without it being an mtf repainter. I use the 21SMA instead of the HA and the 55SMA to resemble M5 action. I also have news and other extras but they are not needed, just additional things that sometimes help with how long to stay in and/or if we should take a secondary entry.

If you want to stay safe and take less trades, only take the 1st instance of the 34 crossing zero while the 144 is already above. The magenta line should have crossed 50 in your direction and everything else is self-explanatory.

There is 1 template with alerts and 1 without and I usually take the 1st PROPER setup after 08 gmt and then the same again after 14 gmt. I trade e/j and g/u and it makes more then enough for this to be my only form of income.

Good trading to you all.

Oh yeah, my final notes would be about some of the negative crap I read on some of this threads pages.

1. This system works if you follow the rules

I'm using an MM approach where i'll cover half my lots after getting 10 pips or cover my SL amount. Then i'll wait til a candle closes past 2:1, where i'll start manually adjusting my stop about 20 pips trailing - first to B/E after 2:1, then everytime it closes another 10 pips away i'll move the stop so its about 20 pips away. Hope this makes sense to everyone. I'm looking to lock in about 10 pips if i can, get to cover b/e and then let the rest ride if possible.

This worked pretty well today. I let some winners ride, and kept the losses small.

--- 帖子 #143 ---
Attached Image (click to enlarge)

The blue candle is formed and we are near a declining 21SMA, which tells us that the bulls are the winners of that 2 minutes but the general direction is down. This means that it is highly probable that we are just seeing a small retrace on the downward movement and just need to wait for the bears to take control again. (which is what I refer to as bear candle eating bull candle)

And so by 'eating', I mean the next candle was taken over by the bears and ate up all the gains that the bulls had made in the previous candle, and more.

We do not have to wait for the candle to close and form any pattern. We simply pull the trigger after the bulls gains are taken away by the bears + an extra 1-2 pips, your call and its all pretty fast anyway.

In the chart I show the 1st trade was triggered and then the bulls jumped in again, this made our entry candle close blue which may confuse some of you a bit, just be aware that at the time of entry it was a red candle and either way showed us that the bears had more power than the bulls because they were able to drive the price down further than the bulls could push it up in an equal space of time (2mins) . The declining 21SMA tells us that momentum is down so once we see the bears overpower the bulls its a good time to enter.

The next 2 entries on that chart are clearer to see since the entry candles close the correct color

Just keep firing the questions if you need more input, its a funny one to put into words

--- 帖子 #158 ---
This is from the text in the indicator. It was written by talkforex

Readme:

I. Features:

This is an improved version of period converter for MT4 based on the

MT4's default period converter by metaquotes.

The default period converter script do not support real-time refreshing,

and consume lots of CPU (50%-9x%) making the whole system slow.

Also, the default one is a script which do not save when you exit MT4,

so you have to apply every converter script again after restarting, quite

annoying.

This one fixed all above problems:

1. Real-time updating or custom interval millisecond level updating.

2. Low CPU cost, average 5%-10% or less.

3. Works as an indicator, so can be saved and reloaded during restart.

4. There is no one converter per chart limitation as it is not script

any more, you can only use one window as source to generate as many

new timeframe chart as possible.

5. Auto updating if there is new history block loaded.

II. How to use:

Copy the mq4 file to your MT4 indicators folder (expertsindicators)

to install it as an indicator, NOT script. then in the custom indicator

list, attach period_converter_opt to the chart you want.

It support 4 parameters:

PeriodMultiplier: new period multiplier factor, default is 2

UpdateInterval: update interval in milliseconds,

zero means update real-time. default is zero.

Enabled: You can disable it without remove it with this option.

Other parameters are comments or for debugging, it is safe to ignore them.

Also Make sure you have Allow Dll imports option checked in common tab or

it won't work

After that, File->Open Offline to open the generated offline data. then

the offline data will be updated automatically.

As long as you keep the source chart open and the converter indicator

running, the generated chart including indicators inside will always

be updated. also you can close the generated chart and open again

later from File->Open Offline without problem.

If you want to quit MT4, you can leave those offline chart as other

normal online charts. when you start MT4 next time, those charts will

also be loaded and updated.

III. Notes:

1. Do NOT uncheck the "offline chart" option in offline chart common properties.

or after MT4 restart, it will treat that chart as online chart and request

the data from server, resulting empty chart window.

2. You can attach more than one converter to same window with different

PeriodMultiplier, e.g: you can attach 3 converter with

PeriodMultiplier = 2, 4, 10 to M1 to generate M2, M4, M10 at the same time.

It is even ok to use the M1 chart to generate Hourly chart like H2, which

only cost a few more CPU resource during initial conversion. but usually

most server don't have much data for those short period. resulting the

generated data isn't long enough for long period. so it is suggested

to use Hourly/Daily charts as source when needed.

3. The real-time updating mode updates quotes as fast as possible, but as

this is done via script, and MT will skip calling start() function when

your PC is busy and lots of quotes income. anyway, this seldom happen,

and you can at least get 10 updates each seconds which is much more

than enough.

4. The offline chart don't have a bid line showing in chart, but all data

in the chart including the indicators is still being updated,

so don't worry. you can show the bid line by unclick the "offline chart"

option in chart properties. but which don't helps much and if you forget

to check "offline chart" option before exit. it will cause errors and

become empty on next startup. you have to close the window and open

again from File->Open offline, which don't worth the trouble.

IV. History:

2005.12.24 1.4 faster to detect if data changed by removing float point

operations, added support to output CSV file in real time.

OutputCSVFile = 0 means no CSV.

OutputCSVFile = 1 means CSV + HST

OutputCSVFile = 2 CSV only, no HST .

(useful if you want to generate CSV for builtin periods)

CSV Filename will be the same as HST file except the extension.

added safe checking for PeriodMultiplier.

2005.12.04 1.3 Fixed missing data when there is large amount of data

loaded in several blocks, and support auto updating

when new history is loaded.

2005.11.29 1.2 Additional fix for missing data and server changing.

2005.11.29 1.1 Fixed missing partial data after restart.

Reinitialize after changing server or data corrupted.

2005.11.28 1.0 Initial release

"Going To Double Or Triple

My Conversion Rate"

ACTION: I went through the copy and gave suggestions on what I would do to improve it, while recording my actions and voice on video. Next I sent the video over to Roger and he made changes as per my suggestions.

RESULT: Roger saw a dramatic increase in his response. In fact, at the rate his conversion is increasing, he expects it to double or triple in days.

Here's What Roger Said About My Copy ...

"I just finished watching the critique that was recorded for me (on video). I'm just blown away.

I was making so many mistakes on my copy. It wasn't converting as much as I wanted it to convert. So I hired Jesse, and he just blew me away. His suggestions are going to double or triple my conversion rate.

His secrets and tactics about the layout, and where things should go on the web page just really blew me away. Jesse is an amazing copywriter, and I'm going to keep using him. Thank you Jesse!"

Roger D.

--- 帖子 #226 ---
Most of those entries are OK but some seem to be off by a couple of candles. In your case you have white and red so I will use those colors to explain,

First you do not need to worry about the recent swing for stops. When a red candle closes at or very near a rising 21SMA, you buy if the very next candle is white passes it by 2 pips, you do not wait for the candle to close, as soon as it passes you hit the trigger, stop loss is 2 pips below the red candle we just passed unless the current candle that we are buying on has a lower low, in which case SL is 2 pips below that.

I use a script for all my entries with hard 25pip stop loss and 50pip take profit, this gets me into the trade safe and no internet or connection faliure can screw me too bad. Once in the position I alter both SL and TP accordingly. With the M2 method SL is nearly always between 8-25pips

Like I said before, M2 gets me my first entry on most moves and on many occassions backup the M1 X50 for 2nd and 3rd entries if they happen. Sometimes they do no happen and 2nd and 3rd entries are signalled only by the M1 which is fine too, it just usually means a bigger SL because with the M1 my SL is the latest swing like you mentioned.

--- 帖子 #227 ---
Those breakout indicators work however you set them up. After plenty of trial and error I have determined that the 4 breakout zones on my chart are of the highest probability for success.

The 2 with stars are by far the best, the other 2 are secondary

ALL +2 GMT

00-02 - Asian session kicks off

*08-10 - London opens

*14-16 - London back from lunch an US opens

19-21 - US back from lunch

The way the indicator works for me is to create a grey zone with those times, then it makes me 2 purple lines that extend for the rest of the day after the grey zone ends. Its a simple breakout method I have been using for some time now. You can zoom out on your chart and see how effective they can be. Used in conjuction with the M1 and M2 methods we have discussed here, its the perfect package. At least for me, everyone will see things their own way though.

--- 帖子 #240 ---
Well played Dan, I didn't want to say anything about win ratio because it may start some people off saying its BS but I too am 100% with picking winning entries for nearly 2 months now, except for 2 stupid trades which I only lost 17pips on . Like you though I only trade a couple of hours morn and eve.

I have found that the secret to these kind of results is taking the 1st 2 REAL setups after 8gmt and then the same again at 14gmt. This is basically in conjuction with the breakout zones on my template. I trade e/j and g/u and by real setups I mean as I described in my 1st ever post here when I also provided the template.

About taking profit, I apply a trailing 15 stop loss immediately, then when I see the SL get to break even I change it to a trailing 25. Then I watch as i arrives at any pivots and see how it reacts, if we are selling for example and we arrive at a pivot and then get a bull candle eating up a bear candle I will take my profit. I do not get greedy and 50-100pips/hr is not usually a problem. When trading full 1.0 lots that makes you pretty damn happy as you eat breakfast.

.2 - ALthough we see different templates here, in fact they have a lot in common, using CCIs and RSI's for example...

We can't progress our "investigation" if we don't try other options within the premises set by the initial fxprime. If we try to "keep it simple" so that we'd make it easy for "newbies", we'd be certainly cutting ourselves room for improvement.

--- 帖子 #254 ---
Don't be a sheep would be my advice, discover and make your own rules based on your personality and risk appetite.

Pick a method you like, read everyones take on it, create your own rules that work for you, demo it for a bit and make sure it works for you. No need to jump in and lose money if you are not final with your method. By this I mean solid rules for TP, SL, Entries, Exits... the full package.

Like I think I said in a previous post, there are plenty of methods that will work out great for some and not for others, its not the method thats at fault but the executioner of the method due to confused and flimsy rules.

Consistancy in any of the 100's of methods out there wll all produce results, some more, some less, its your money, your choice.

I used the f4cmnet setup this morning with good success.  While it requires patience I don't see how you can avoid picking up 50 pips within a few trades.   Here are the entry rules as I use them.  I'm going to add the 50 sma to see if that helps with any bad signals.   I was on the 1M chart

For exit I just picked a number of pips I was happy with.   I don't know what f4's exit rules are.  I hope he's back soon to continue sharing his contributions.

Cheers!

Sandy

Long

1.  89/21 cci over 0

2.  stochastic cross with green line above 50

3   heiken ashi turns white

4.  !!MA turns green

4.  QQE line above 50 (my addition)

Short

1.  89/21 cci under 0

2.  stochastic cross with green line under 50

3   heiken ashi turns red

4.  !!MA turns red

4.  QQE line below50 (my addition)

1. Wait for a very specific cross of 3 Moving averages....(I presume it has something to do with moving average angles)

3. Enter the trade when those two things happen (green-buy) (Red-Sell)
(do not blindly trade the green and red....wait for breaks of near support or resistance)

--- 帖子 #327 ---
I have to agree, out with indicators.

I've been an intraday live trader using higher timeframes for a few years, and I decided to increase my forex income scalping lower TFs. I thought maybe i needed a "system"... Well, after 2 months testing, the best system is candles, channels, resistance and support lines!

Know the pair you're trading well, draw some fibs over last swings to watch where retraces will stop, and you're there. Anything with indicators just gives you late signals and because we're working with small profits, can cut your overall number of profits a lot.

Lower timeframes scalping can't be done effectivly with indicators, it's all in PA and knowing where key points are.

I may be wrong in some points, but this is what i've come in to conclusion after these two months testing. And don't get me wrong, i did have overall profit, but i felt and came to be sure of that with indicators i could never take full advantage of this trading technique.

I'll keep lurking around!

--- 帖子 #339 ---
Ahem, anyway, lets get back to biz..to those who download my templates and EA, those gridlines, if you noticed, identify ROUND NUMBERS...1.6000, 1.6050, 1.7000...and so on....Those gridlines are like pivot points. Market price tend to gravitate to the next or before round numbers. Th ADR refers to the average daily range for a particular currency pair. So if the ADR is 180, i may target a 60 pips profit for that pair. You will also notice 6 time frames on the upper left of the chart specially programmed for this system. If you see a green colour time frame, it shows a bull run for that particular time frame. If its red, then a bear is dominating the fall. If no color then the market is indecisive yet. Ofcos with this basic tools WILL NOT make you rich but i'm sure you will capture 20 pips or more just by following the basic rules of the buaya puteh (mighty gator).....

Long

Bear candle eaten by 2 pips

CCI 34 is blue (above 0)

21SMA is blue (rising)

Optional: If near a pivot, it should be breaking it or bouncing off it.

Short

Bull candle eaten by 2 pips

CCI 34 is red (below 0)

21SMA is red (declining)

Optional: If near a pivot, it should be breaking it or bouncing off it.

4 line 34 pips from the 28

7 line 144 pips from the 28.

On the Eur/Usd in a sideways market price will bounce aroudn the 1st and 2nd line. The 28 is

the center of gravity price always reverts back to it.  I wait for it to hit the 3rd or 4th in a sideways market and put on two positions. stop goes above the 3rd or 4th line.  half comes off at the 28 ema. --- 帖子 #417 ---
I'll just give you a quick yes on that one, candle eating candle must be side by side. Its the psychology behind it that got me into this.

ie. In a 2 minute period lets say the bulls gained (x) pips but then in the very next 2 minute period (an equal amount of time is what I'm getting at here because this does work on the M5 also but with bigger SL's) the bears took it all back and more. This shows me that at this moment the bears have more power, and so we then use the 21SMA as a point price always returns to. I'm sure you could use any MA you like for this, the 21 is what I like though.

For those interested I will set-up the M2 thread on Sunday.

--- 帖子 #502 ---
I have to say the old FX-P thread, and this thread have been a wealth of information, and great indicators!

Over the last year, I've tried out zillions of indicators (at least) and one conclusion I've come to is that most of them are telling you the same thing, just in different visual ways.  Some of them show you exactly the same thing.... for instance, a 50-period cci histogram looks exactly the same as a 5/35/5 macd histogram, which looks exactly the same as a Bollinger Squeeze histogram with the right settings..... and the i-Trend indicator is almost identical to the +DI/-DI lines in the ADX indicator, etc, etc. And we all know by now that the cci lines correspond to moving averages. The trick is to find a good combination that tells you what you need to know with a fairly quick look at the chart. And I'm sure different visual methods will work better for some people and worse for others.

So after lots of trial and error and learning a LOT from these FX-Prime and FX-50 threads, I've come up with a visual look that has really helped me, not only how to spot good upcoming trades but how to stay out of the bad ones.  (I wasn't really very impressed with the v2 filter)

I've also discovered I really like Laguerre a lot better than regular RSI. It seems to be much less choppy and easier to read (I use .85 setting, not the standard). I've also discovered that for me, personally (and this could just have to do with the way I interpret what I'm seeing), it doesn't help much to try to stay inside the larger trend (like the cci89 or cci170). I find it's kind of six-of-one, half-a-dozen of the other whether you try to stay with those trends or not, because they change frequently (particularly on 1-minute charts), and a lot of really good moves start on the other side of the trend that you would miss.

Anyway, have attached a chart with a visual method that has been working for me. The icing on the cake was the instant trendline indicator that was just posted (thanks!!).  I tried it out with my chart and it just brought it all together.

The rules are really simple...

Look for a very tight rainbow twist, which must be INSIDE the red and blue trendlines. At the same time, Laguerre must be crossing up .25 (for a buy) or crossing down .75 (for a sell), the 55cci must be crossing 0, and Kino's buycount must change to the right color. The tighter the twist, the better the signal (some of these on GBP/JPY end up being 300+ moves).

The key is the twist.... if the 3 lower indicators on the bottom are all saying "go" but it's a very loose twist or it's outside the lines of the red and blue trendlines, don't do it.  And if you do have a tight twist inside the lines, but laguerre is not in the right place or any of the other indicators don't match up, don't do it.

Exit when laguerre goes the other way (crossing down thru .75 or up through .25) and the trendlines have crossed.

If the trade goes against you, you'll know it because you'll get a reversal signal, either with the rainbow twist, or laguerre, etc.

Laguerre seems to be the strongest indicator for knowing when to get out.  Sometimes there are other exit signals, like cci crossing 0, trendlines crossing, etc, but if laguerre is still a flat line on the top or bottom, it's almost always better to stay in.

I don't really use ADX for entries or exits, but a) it's just an extra indication of trend and strength of trend (the red/green lines are almost identical to i-Trend) and b) if the yellow ADX line is below 23, then there is little momentum and if you are already in a trade and and it's not going the way you want and worried if you should exit, it's probaby better to hold and wait and see what happens if ADX is below 23.

In the attached chart, the first two yellow vertical lines show possible entries... in the first one, the trendlines have crossed and the 3 indicators are all saying "Sell" (laguerre, cci crossing 0 and buycount changed to red). But it was a loose twist and not inside the trendlines, so not a good signal.

The second yellow line also shows a pretty tight rainbow twist but a) it's not inside the trendlines and b) laguerre is not in the right place.  So it's not a good signal.

The green vertical shows a nice tight twist inside the red and blue trendlines and all systems are go down below, with laguerre crossing down through .85, cci crossing 0, kino buycount changed to red, and as an added bonus, the red/green lines in ADX have crossed and spread apart, and the yellow ADX line is moving up to show added momentum. Perfect exit when trendlines crossed, laguerre passed up thru .25, cci crossed 0 and buycount changed to green, total about 115 pips.  The exit signal was also a possible entry signal.... the twist wasn't really tight enough so I probably would have passed on it, but it turned out to be a +50 move.

Zip file with indi's and template attached, if anyone wants it....

All standard settings except laguerre is .85 and I use cci55.

--- 帖子 #507 ---
I added the gSpeak file to the zip file, also one additional template (and indicator) that uses different lines than the Instant Trend lines and removes one set of the rainbow mma's.

I think it might work slightly better that way.  Another tip is that when looking at the charts, the best signals come when the trend lines cross and create a 45 degree angle, and the twist is centered in it as much as possible.  If the trend lines create a very wide angle, it's not good. I know it's sometimes hard to tell when it's first forming, though.

Of the three possible entries in this chart... the first one is a really loose twist and totally off-center from the trendline cross.  The second one was a better twist but somewhat off-center, and the indicator signals didn't line up. They should really line up at the same time, and in this case, laguerre crossed up two or three bars before cci.  The next trendline cross and twist had laguerre in the middle so I wouldn't look at that one.  Once in a while you will see a good trade with laguerre in the wrong place, but overall it's a lot safer to wait for it to be right.  There will also be times where there are some really good moves that started with a very loose twist, too, but much better to avoid them the vast majority of the time.

So the third (green) entry in this one was pretty close to perfect.... super-tight twist, centered between the trend lines, which created pretty close to a 45 degree angle (even pointing 45 degrees down, toward the lower-left corner.... as you go back through the charts the best ones actually seem to point at 45 degrees, either toward the lower right for a sell, or the upper right for a buy, although sometimes it's hard to tell when it's first forming).  That one went on to be +143 pips (GBP/JPY).

Sorry, the entry rules were not posted as I had thought, I have been in this system early on from the other ( ahem) thread so, I base my entry loosely on that system.

However, if you look at the charts you can clearly see where it suggests you enter and exit.

These are the rules from the previous thread.

FINAL ENTRY SIGNAL RULES (NOT ON THE POST BELOW FOLLOW THIS HERE!)

Long Trade

CCI 170 Over the 0 Line showing uptrend MUST BE THE FIRST TO CROSS

CCI 34 Over 0 line as well showing uptrend MUST BE SECOND TO CROSS IN SAME DIRECTION

RSI over 55 <------ VERY IMPORTANT dont enter if its in between the 45-55 zone (45-55) IS DANGER DO NOT ENTER ZONE once it crosses in the same direction take the trade.

Short Trade
CCI 170 under 0 line showing down trend MUST CROSS FIRST

CCI 34 under 0 line showing down trend MUST CROSS SECOND

RSI under 45 same as above dont trade when in the 45-55 zone

**VERY IMPORTANT**

NEVER TRADE AGAINST THE 5 MIN TREND, IF ITS TRENDING DOWN AND ITS GIVING YOU AN UP SIGNAL DONT TAKE IT ITS A RETRACEMENT WHEN IT COMES DOWN AGAIN TAKE THE SIGNAL. LOOK FOR LOWER LOWS AND HIGHER HIGHS...

Having some time on my hands I decided to take the 1M - 2M -5M & 15M time frames and do a comparison with identical entry and exit criteria for a random pick of the day last week ( 1 day only - cause it's a lot of work) based on the scalping method f4 and I use which is almost identical. He uses a couple of indicators I don't use, and I use a couple he doesn't - but all in all our systems are pretty close to one another. I was just curious which time frame would be better with my (our) strategy because I get burned out on the 1M.

Interesting results. I compared the time frames from starting at 3:00am GMT all the way to the market closing. Granted - 1 day's comparison does NOT mean it will be identical every day - but nonetheless I found the results informative and leads to ending some speculation on my part about the effectiveness of our strategy on various scalping time frames.

The profit or loss figures have had the brokerage spreads already figured in.

In essence, this is the results of that one day comparison: G/U

15M time frame: 5 trades (3 losses). Daily profit 35 pips

5M: 11 trades (2 losses = 82% win rate) Daily profit 220 pips.

2M: 25 trades (6 losses = 76% win rate) Daily profit 549 pips.

1M: 43 trades (12 losses = 72% win rate) Daily profit of 849 pips.

I had a string of 7 losses on the 1m starting around 19:00hrs GMT, but two good winners right afterwards before the market closed gained me pips over those losers.

P.S.  I don't consider a system or test valid unless I can do it live, which was the case here.  In the past whenever I'd do a backtest I noticed that after awhile I'd look at the trend in general and I'd subsconsciously change my exit or entry points, which actually negated the results of my testing.  So this comparison was done minute by minute.

--- 帖子 #545 ---
The original V1 settings for the Double Woodies CCI was 34/170. Included in the V1 system were the HAS candles and an RSI setting of 14. This worked well and there was nothing wrong with it in total. It made me a bundle and got my scalping profitable.

I, as a personal choice replaced the RSI with the QQE Alert because it gave the identical value information as the RSI but it gave me the benefit of having an alert when the QQE crossed the 50 line. So no dramatic changes had occurred up to this point.

Soon I, like f4 and some others saw that we preferred not to sit and wait so long for the 34CCI to cross ’0’ back into the 170. We saw that while it may have been riskier (and that is open to debate) we were wanting to get into trades sooner and hitting an extra 10+ pips. I changed the Woodies Double CCI almost back to Woodies (not CD’s) original settings and that worked better for me with my psychological trading barriers.

F4 also felt the same way and did a better change than mine by just changing the original settings of 34/170 to 21/89. Plus he added 2 Guppy lines with the values of 35/55 and traded price action bounces off those two guppy lines. I liked what he was doing there so I started including them on my charts. Eventually we both replaced his 35/55 guppy lines with 12 (or 14) and 25 guppy lines as it was more accurate for trading the bounces on the 1M we felt.

And CunuckCT along with a couple of others tweaked and helped support the original V1 system along the way in so many ways I couldn’t begin to mention here. Conversely others came in and starting adding on superfluous, unreliable and untested indicators that certainly didn’t help improve the accuracy of the original system.

In regards to V2’s accuracy and profit potential you are faced with the same situation as occurred in the original V1 thread. V2 was ‘created’ using the new ‘improved filter’ which was alleged to keep one out of 90% of the bad trades. Before judgment can be passed on it’s effectiveness one must remember that CD (or whoever actually designed the V2) did so with his original Double Woodies CCI settings of 34/170. So to make an accurate comparison if V2 DOES work effecively you have to keep the 34/170CCI V1 values in mind, and not the CCI changes made by me or others.

We are NOT all the same. If we were, one system, one or two identical indicators, one time frame would work for all of us and we’d all be millionaires. Sad to say this is not the case is it?

Gasgas’s recent posting about the 10 pips is SO RIGHT ON! And let me explain why. When I did that recent almost 24 hour marathon time frame comparison I was surprised by the results, as I had anticipated the outcome to be different. But what it showed that ‘scalping’ CAN be profitable any time throughout the day. Yes, there are times when a trading session is ‘more’ profitable.

I ‘m after 500 pips a day. BUT I DON’T EXPECT THAT! What I expect (and in all honesty I have to keep reminding myself of this) is to get 10 PIPS! That’s it! That’s my goal! I’m scalping! I’m not looking for a bunch of indicators to line up and show me the way to a 40+ trend move. If it happens (which it does frequently) great! But it happens when I’m after my 10 pip profit and I’ll ride the trade until my indicators or candles tell me to get out. And yes I do trade 3 to 5 lots for my total daily goal.

Once again, I’m after a 10 pip profit. Then I’m after that again, and again, and again. I think my point is made here. And if all I make for the whole day is 10 pips . . . . I’m OK and happy with that!

P.S. And fxtrading24 and rodhuy are correct. Keep this thread dealing with V1 and/or V2. If someone wants to change something or add other indicators at least have the courtesy to demo trade those changes for awhile. Then post them along with an explanation of how those indicators are better, the reasons you changed them, and exactly what they've done to improve your scalping. That would be so much more beneficial to the rest of us! Celticheart did a classic job of that in HER posting!

--- 帖子 #623 ---
I have been experimenting with this some myself and I think I have a good idea of how to explain these signals. (correct me if I'm wrong)

When MA13(Red Line) and MA7(Green Line) are both above or below MA50(Cyan Line) in the same direction AND you have a GREEN(Buy) or a RED(Sell) signal on your FXPrimeV2 "Filter" is your "true" entry signal.

Your Exit signal is the Cross of MA13(Red Line) and MA7(Green Line).  So if MA7(Green Line) crosses above MA13(Red Line) that is when you exit a SELL, when MA13(Red Line) crosses above MA7(Green Line) is when you exit a BUY.

So if you look at the attached chart below hopefully you will see what I describe.  The section you have described as a false signal would have been exited earlier then you have indicated; which would have netted some pips.

--- 帖子 #631 ---
FXP V2 uses more indicators to filter out bad cross trades ...  all the blue dots are BAD Signals that FX Prime V1 would give...  when you see these dots stay out of the market!!!  When you see green solid bar you BUY when you see a solid red line you SELL but only at the right time of the day or night.

It's as simple as that...  question is when is the right time to trade?  I think from 3:00 AM Est to 11:00 AM Est.

--- 帖子 #696 ---
I use a bit different setup, and Laguerre is very helpful, but sometimes you can't avoid the false signals.

In my chart, I also look for a tight twist of the rainbow-colored ma's and for them to be centered between the purple ma's.  This is what I use as my "filter," and what I check last after the other indi's say to enter (being Laguerre .85 and cci55).

In the first entry, I probably would not have taken it because a) the twisting ma's were off-center from the purple ones and b) if you look back in the chart a ways, it looks like the uptrend just recently started after quite a long downtown, so it was probably just a retracement.  However, that one was more tricky, i *might* have taken it.  I also use ADX and though I don't usually use it for entries, in that case, the red adx line was starting to pass through the yellow adx line, meaning the downtrend was weakening, so just another indication that it was an "iffy" signal. But the main thing that would have caused me to pause there would have been the rainbow ma's outside of the purple ones.

The second entry was totally filtered out by my ma's.... the purple lines didn't even cross and the rainbow lines were outside of them. Plus Laguerre was moving back up.

*However*.... that second dip down just before the up-move... i might have taken that one.  Nothing is perfect.

--- 帖子 #710 ---
I fully agree you can profit taking all the signals of a system.

My point is don't think that a system doesn't work if you get some signals that hit a SL. If taking all the signals you make more pips than you loose, the system works.

It's better to have 10 good trades of 10 pips each, and 5 bad of -5 pips; than have 4 good trades of 2 pips and 0 bad trades.

I saw a poll asking if you thought there was a 100% win ratio system.

Well, there is:  No SL, unlimited money, 1 pip TP at a time. If the trade is open, the system has not failed

When both MAs are trending... up or down....then we'd better get ready to gain some pips or more....

My 2 cts.

--- 帖子 #762 ---
Hi All

Great scalping thread you have here. Congrats!!

Here is my two cents contribution. If you overlay CCI_MA_Smoothed.mq4 on top of DoubleWoodyCCI you can even more clearly pinpoint your entry en exit.

I use settings 89, 21 on DoubleWoodyCCI and my CCI inputs on CCI_MA_Smoothed are 21, 0, 30.

I have also tried the DoubleWoodyCCI introduced by CanuckCT (post 66), however overlay doesn't succeed with that one the way it should be..... exactly fitting.

There is a snag with all overlays, for sometimes you may notice that both indicators are not 100% synchronized. Shifting the chart a little to the right or to left most of the time solves that......

Maybe KINO who is the specialist here in overlays and synchronization would just be so kind to add the SMA to the DoubleWoodyCCI ..... (For that is what is actually all about here) because that would solve the shift problem...... that sometimes (rarely though) may occur.

BTW the CCI_MA_Smoothed.mq4 is used in other Scalping systems with great succes for entry and exit.

Cheers, John

--- 帖子 #763 ---
john nice indicator, but why would u over lay them, i'm seeing using one or the other, but stacking both defeats the whole purpose of the double cci. if your trading that cci 21 cross of sma , then why even have the 89 trend cci there, not bad for exits though. just asking because i'm not understanding the stack just yet. does look like a earlier entry, but earlier is not always safest entry and I would be entering with out confemation of the entry from the dual cci which this system is set up around, I haven't looked back at it's signal enough, but being early could get you bit in the ass on 0 line rejects, plus those early entries don't jive with anything eles on my chart set up to support the double CCI

--- 帖子 #764 ---
You're right...... It's just that the SMA gives an earlier signal that a possible entry is at hand shown by the DoubleWoody in the FX-50 system. Validity of entries of course should be handled by FX-50 system rules.... Nothing new there!!!!

However, f.i. when a long trade has been started you will notice that the 89 CCI (gray line) is above the SMA and stays there until exit.... unless you decide for an ealier exit when the yellow CC 21 crosses the SMA.

In this way it gives (some) guidance not to exit too early and certainly not too late either.

Another advantage though is that it makes exit posiblities more visual. Anyway that's what I like most about it.

BTW Have al ook at both CCI-MA-Smoothed and ZLS and you'll notice a remarkable ressemblance there also..... So if KINO could put it together the way I described in my previous post...... it's possible to leave the ZLS away..... which saves space in the chart.

John

--- 帖子 #766 ---
I love it to be a junior here on the forum (for my age is 62)) and I am trading for more than 20 years, Stocks, options and nowadays only FOREX.

Okay having said that...... on to the remark I'd like to make. Basically the FX-50 system is a Wave 5 (Elliot waves therory) trading system, for most of time time the Wave 3 is being skipped here by the CCI 89/21 setup.

Nothing wrong with that..... That is just how this system works. But when you are quite good at divergencies you will also be able to take the Wave 3 trades..... These most of the time happen when the CCI 21 crosses the zero line first.

An example of that just happened now on EURUSD with the short trade entry possibility of 11:48 GMT. Yellow 21 one coming down first crossing zeroline..... Next Gray 89 coming down after under SMA at 11:48 GMT

Next you do is lean back and wait for the gray line to get above the SMA..... Presently it's on a 60 pips ride already.....

But indeed you should only do this when you know all the ins and outs about divergencies/convergencies signalling boost potential at entry points.

Notwithstanding the foregoing if you stick to the FX-50 rules the SMA comes in quite handy too with the DoubleWoodyCCI.

Cheers, John

--- 帖子 #795 ---
Ok here it is

What you see on the chart is three Gann HILO Activators that I mainly use for entry verifiation (Red one) and support/resistance, which are the other two...... 1 used on TF5 and 1 on TF15.

You have to get used a bit to the stepping indicators.... for they refresh until the moment of closing.... TF5 every 5 minutes.... TF15 every 15 minutes. So they do not repaint after closing of the last step...... only refresh during their respective 5 minute and 15 minute cycle. In this way they also act as Dynamic Support/Resistance levels.

You need the ex4 file of the Gann HILO Activator..... Couldn't find the right mq4 file for this so far....

The Yellow T3MA (40) is sort of a mediator. I never go short above it and never go long under it...... In that it does show some ressemblance with the CCI 89 periods above and under zero...... If this T3MA is crossing the pricefield...... the chart is in whipsaw area. I see that as NTZ's.... No Trading Zones.

BTW you'll always notice when it comes together with Spudfibo lines there is increased resistance or support. T3MA shrtly overhead limits to the upside -resistance. T3MA shortly under the pricefield limits to the downside - support.

The signal indicator is a 2 MA crossover, that I use with Stealth Company settings.... works exactly the same or better as their Early Bird. You may want to change the MA periods..... but I advise not to change the MA Types !!

I assume you all have the #Spudfibo..... therefore it's not included in the list below. Also not included are the DoubleWoodieCCI and CCI_MA_Smoothed that you can find at post #767.

Good luck, John

I am not a creative thinker like so many here are, and as much as I dislike Rastaman I'll give the devil his due and state he, like many others has contributed a lot to this thread!

All I have done is taken CD's original system, took out a couple of his indicators and added one or two I liked in exchanged, and it made me (and still is) a bundle. Plus it opened me up to being a successful scalper which fit my personality. I hated and was bored everyday trading 1hr TF up. It made me money, but I wasn't having fun until scalping on the 1M started being exciting and rewarding.

All I am is a stubborn Scotsman. I found something that I liked, tweaked it a little, and when I would have a losing day I didn't throw the system in the garbage and search for something better on another thread. I evaluated what I had done wrong and why, and sometimes, flat-out I hadn't done anything wrong. It was just the way the market moved that time, or that day. I stayed with the system, got to know it better, and work it better, and didn't abandon it for a 'Holy Quail' elsewhere which would turn into a turkey in time

There is absolutely nothing wrong with having a thread evolve and become better. But when so many different things are added (most of which are nothing more than attempts to re-invent the wheel) and indicators added without the slightest knowledge OR experience with those indicators, then you don't have evoluation, you simply have confusion!

I had my rant against Rastaman, and I've forgotten about it already. But me not posting here anymore is just because I'm (contrary to this post) not going to clutter up a thread with anything which fails to compliment that thread or help someone understand the system better. You have a lot of smart people here contributing, far smarter than I am. Problem is, you'll never keep the dumb ones out.

But V1 (and I guess for some V2) works well. I want my charts simple, clean, uncluttered with only one or two indicators that I know work well and gives me instant information I want from different mathematical analysis to pull the trigger or not. Which means I would be handicapping myself if I had to look at a bunch of indicators and evaluate what each one was telling me, and mostly what I see posted are people throwing a whole bunch of indicators on their charts which don't reveal any pertinent information, but just identical information present only graphically different. I'm scalping, and sometimes those first few moments are critical about getting in a trade early enough to make some pips, and get out when it's clear it's going to turn against me, and most important riding the hot trend for boucoup pips.

I can't say it any other way anymore, which is why I am not posting here anymore. V1 works. f4 and others changed things that made it better. But even in the original format, it worked, and it worked well.

I'm not leaving this thread pissed, I'm just leaving and going back trading. Just don't have the time or inclination to keep up with all the postings. If I felt I had something earth-shattering to share I'd stay. But truthfully, I really don't![/quote]

--- 帖子 #915 ---
I found the FXprime_V2 Final.mq4 to be a bit slow, whereas it is using the CD almost original settings for CCI, i.e. 170/50. The templates we use in this thread however all are implemented on fxtrading24's new FX-50 system and now is using CCI 89/21.

For that reason I have been fiddling the settings of FXprime_V2 Final.mq4 to get it more responsive to the main indicator in the templates presently used in this thread.

Especially those of you using the SoEasy template will notice the difference at a glance. What you could do is place it in a second window underneath for a while for comparison..... If you dont like it...... just throw it away again....

My first impression is that " some bad trades" that would hardly get you the required number of pips to make that specific trade worth wile are better filtered now too....

Anyway here are the changed settings and see how it works for you:

CCI_period = 63

Long_period = 64

EMA_period= 36

Start EMA Shift = 0

EndEMAShift = -21     (don't forget the minus sign !!)

That's all......

Another thing is to stop this indicator shifting up and down.... you can do this in the Meta Editor and leave away /* and */ when you see this

/*

#property indicator_minimum -100

#property indicator_maximum 100

*/

Next recompile and shifting wil stop.

You can also change this at the Common Tab of the indicator (when you change the other settings) and enter Fixed minimum = -100 and Fixed Maximum = 100

Good luck and may all of you have a nice day, John

--- 帖子 #953 ---
C'mon...there must be some advice you can provide for when to trade and when to stand aside when scalping.

Here is chart that I would submit for starting a discussion. Is there anything obvious about it?

Well...we had a nice uptrend for the first part of the week....a reversal and finished right back where we started the week. What does this mean for next week....we'll see how it handles the low around 1.4812.

Throughout the week you could draw trendlines to represent what price might do to create a new trend, extend an existing trend...or range, while it decides what to do. No indicators can tell you this....it's pure price action. And I understand how the indicators help to pull the trigger...I use of version of FX-50 for M1. For M2, M5 and M15...it's pretty much pure price action.

So when you sit down to trade, before you do anything....load an M15 chart....zoom out and draw some trendlines...see if it helps you in your M1 trading.

It's near these threndlines that you start to get signals from systems. This is why sometimes price bounces for no apparent reason...and sometimes when you trade it turns immediately against you...cause you are doing exactly the opposite of the 5% who are getting it right.

It might be offtopic for scalping....but it does help to assess where the critical areas are and when you might be ranging and why. When you break these trendlines...the system signals are the ones you want to take.

Timeframe is M15 for GU for the week.

Cheers

CanuckCT

--- 帖子 #1004 ---
Monster,

I will attempt to briefly answer some of your questions, I can assure you based on the pic you posted that you need to dial back on some of the indicators. Try to understand the basics of this system, after you have a grasp on the basics then add additional indicators one at a time to see if they enhance your trading.

1 - I'm only using this on the 1 min tf. So I haven't installed any of the 5 min indicators....is this correct?

The original system called for a double woodies CCI 170 & 34 on the 5min and 1min charts. A valid trade required the CCI 170 to cross before the CCI 34 on the 1 min chart, with the CCI 170 in both the 1min and 5min chart either above or below zero. Once the CCI 34 crossed in the direction of the CCI 170, you also need and RSI above 55 or below 45.

2- The ccidoublewoody that comes in the zip file has pre sets to 14 and 6, while the guide has two different presents of 170 & 34, and 21 & 89. Which is correct? Also what about the one with RSI? which is the most valid?

170 & 34 was the original, 21 & 89 is a latter modification. You will have to test which one better fits your still of trading. You will find various RSI settings from 14 to 8, again you have to do some work and determine what works for you.

I've found that if I change the original 'New FX50' settings to 21 & 89, they correspond the closest with the Heiken Ashi color changes

3- I found that a few of the indicators give counter signals to one another ie: Bollinger squeeze V stock 513 vs double cc1

once again some indicators will enhance the 170/34, while others work better with 89/21. Once again you have to do some testing.

4 - I noticed my Kino all in one v2 has different color setups than the one in the guide.

Kino is a great guy and kicks out indicators like an assembly line, and even have various revisions to specific indicators. Once again you must determine what works for you.

My last statement isn't meant to be mean or cynical, but becoming a successful forex trader requires a lot of work. Studying, technical analysis, and testing. Many times new traders, want to be spoon feed - it does nothing for your personal growth (now maybe you aren't a new trader, but an experienced trader should have no problems developing a logical approach to testing the information provided over the three individual threads). Even when someone gives most new traders a winning system they still lose money, why? A good system is just your edge, and one component of being a successful trader. If you don't understand the basic concepts behind the indicators and the system its unlikely that you will have continued success and we all dont process the same information in the same manner.

Start with just the HA candles, DoubleCCI, and RSI. Learn the interaction of these 3 indicators first and make adaptations from there.

This is just my opinion

Dallas

--- 帖子 #1018 ---
I backtested FXPrime v1 and v2 both with the same exit CCI crosses 0 with the mt strategy tester.

My results show that the original v1 is the most profitable.

Main difference between the 2 systems is that v2 also takes trades where trend cci follows entry cci, whereas in the original v1 trend cci must cross 0 before entry cci.

V2 tries to compensate too many false signals besides other mechanisms with the ma-filter, that says, that an ma cross in trade direction should happen shortly before the trade. That improves the results of v2 without ever reaching v1 results. v1 results don't improve with such an ma filter.

I would recommend to trade original v1 with entry cci 34 following trend cci 170 and with one additional filter condition: trend cci should be > 100 for buys and < 100 for sells. This condition showed the best results.

A 89-21-cci-system turned out to be even less profitable than v2. I have not tested f4mnect's guppy bounces.

--- 帖子 #1033 ---
1M bouncing can be easily regconise using belows setting:

1) Storch RSI

2) BOL 18

3) Tor ADX

Buy condition:

1) Closing pprice bar is crossing over BOL lower band

2) closing price is lesser then opening price(it means RED bar)

3) buy when previous Storch RSI <=1 and current previous Storch RSI > 1

4) ADX for 5M showing BUY (blue)

exit when Storch reach 70 or up to your own judgement.

SL always 20 pip for EU.

Sell condition is vice versa.

SoEasy,

This is a question I just have to ask after weeks of seeing you post this stuff. My simple question is why???? Please dont take this as an attack, but I just dont see any logical purpose behind it. You admit that you don't trade either V1 or V2 live - so what is the purpose. Granted everyone has an opinion, but this thread is about instruction and instruction implies execution, and showing moves after the fact, that were never executed has very little instructional value, IMHO. But hey, I can be wrong because I also believe that demo trading and back testing also has limited value.

My mantra is if you think something works, than start loading up 3 lot or lot equivalent shots on a live account, you will figure out very quickly whether the system works for you or even has potential.

--- 帖子 #1092 ---
Learn V1 is much more reliable if you trade by the rules. V2 is a good system, but you need some trading experience to avoid losses.

In the old V1 thread RonaldRaygun made an ea that most used for signals. I still use it since I trade from work and I can't be watching my laptop at all times. I am not an ea programmer, but I changed its original settings (170-34) to 89/21 that most of us are using now. Download the ea and install in your MT Experts folder, then drag it to your chart and set it to: Signals Only: True - Alerts: True - Play Sounds: True - Use Times: False

You can leave the other settings as they are or change them as you please. You can even let it trade for you or close the trades, but I wouldn't recommend it.

Again, don't just trade any signal and try not to trade when market is moving slow or ranging.

...............

for each indicator macd , cci , sma etc... and each TF

green is abobe (zero or close or limit you can fix)

red is below

for RSI & ADX :

when color = yellow  >> the conditions are not good ;examples :

ADX is under value 25 (or else) yellow , if green = buy , red = sell

RSI is in the (zone 45/55) : yellow , if green = buy , red = sell

Excuse my asking but what is happening when your broker only allows you to use charts with an "m" at the end of the currency pair.  I noticed that the spread is much wider than when the "m" is not there.  Is there a reason behind this, my broker is IBFX.

--- 帖子 #1136 ---
M means mini account, ibfx does not have fixed spreads so that means spreads can change and go up during high volatility markets, such as news, and very high volume. The m has nothing to do wit it other than it means mini account.

--- 帖子 #1152 ---
OK. Here is how I changed the sidewinder expiration date.

When you have your sidewinder in the MT4 application, you open up the MetaQuotes Language Editor and select the sidewinder. Then you scroll down until you see the picture below and change the year that is set from 2006 to whatever date you want (2010 and up). Then you close it and save it and it should work.

D.

--- 帖子 #1212 ---
Hey, guys...

do any of you know how to program an audible/popup alert for the T3 RSI, when the rsi line crosses the T3 line?

That is my main indicator now so an audible alert would be great... been working quite well for me on a live account.  I use a 100 period T3 and if the T3 crosses on the same bar as a 5/12ema cross (or no more than 2 bars away) then I take the trade.  Exit at the next T3 cross.  I also have 21 and 50 emas on the chart to show the larger trend (love that ma ribbon filled indicator!), but don't use it for entries or exits. (I have two filled ma ribbons, one with 21/50 ema's and one with 5/12 ema's and an indicator with arrows to show when the 5/12ema's actually cross)

If the T3 crosses several bars before or after a 5/12ema cross then it's not a good signal.  The T3 line also gives a good indication of trend depending whether it's above 55/below 45 and starting to go the other way.

I've also noticed that when e/u and g/u are going well, the yen crosses are choppy and vice versa, so I trade the e/u while it's doing well, then if it starts getting choppy and the trades don't work out I switch over to a/j or e/j to see how they're doing.  I also set a breakeven stop after +20 pips or so, just in case

(actually, a 150 period T3 might be even a bit better.. the good signals correspond pretty well with the signals from the 100 T3, but it seems to filter a few of the false ones. I may keep both on the chart for a while to compare.)

--- 帖子 #1262 ---
OK. As you know, playing with the 1min chart is a very risky thing to do, that's why most traders go with the 5 or 15min chart. That filters out some of the false signals. The different systems or templates that you could get or have already from the V1 and now V2 versions give some good signals on the 1 min chart. On the 5 min chart those signals are a little bit safer. I also would recommend that you trade only the European session that goes into the US session. The times I like to trade is start 1hr before European session starts and stop 2hr before it ends. This is where you get the most out of the session.

You have to decide on which time frame you wanna trade, 1min or 5 min. You can not avoid false signals all the time. Get to know your charts. I hate to say that but get a feeling for the chart you wanna trade and you will be a better trader in the long run.

Today for example, the GBP/USD and the EUR/USD were very choppy and it was hard to get a good signal. When you recognize that this happens, you just switch to another currency. EUR/JPY for example had some very well signals to trade for.

Alright e` then.

D.

(Forexweasel)I look at the chart and see the candles and what they look like. If you see that the candles have an irregular flow (I would say), what I mean by that is that the body is to long, the shadows on both end are unusual long or short. Or look at the 5min chart. If there is the same irregularity as in the 1 min or even worse, then don't trade. A great example right now is the GBP/USD, just look at the candlesticks.

--- 帖子 #1290 ---
Sure - here it is. Start on page 7.
http://www.nexgent3.com/T-3%20Fibs%2...%202-28-08.pdf

But be careful right now. Just about the time you get a nice little trend going it turns quickly back into a killer chop. The way I use the BBMACD is (mostly) I wait for it to cross the 0 line. Dots HAVE to be outside the channel. When a dot changes colors and ducks back into the channel I exit. If I feel conservative I do not buy when it's below the '0' (even if the dots are green) nor do I enter a sell trade ABOVE the '0' if the dots are red. To be clearer, I only sell when dots are red and below the '0', and I only buy if dots are green and ABOVE the '0'.

I use the QQE mtfv5 for a 50 cross alert only, although I think it is also a great indicator and can almost stand alone. My candle chart I only use the xpMA along with a 15EMA. Attaching a chart in a minute so you can see what I mean.

P.S. The dots repaint ONLY on the current dot.

--- 帖子 #1296 ---
I can only give you my opinion and what works or doesn't work for me. No, I don't use the 45/55 as a filter. I don't believe filters even exist that work and I could give you a thousand examples of why I came to believe that. It's like I constantly hear traders wanting to go to a higher time frame 'to eliminate noise.'

You NEVER eliminate noise. You go to a 30M tf, then you have noise from the 5m & the 15m. Go to a weekly tf, you've got noise from the daily, or the 4H time frame. And it goes on and on. See what I mean?

I can see the value of the 45/55 channel on the RSI, but on the QQE I wanna know the instant it crosses the 50. That is basically my 'filter'. ANd THAT even bites me in the butt a lot because I constantly see trades where I would have made boucoup more pips had I entered the trade when the two QQE lines crossed REGARDLESS where it was in conjunction to the 50 line. But I also see many times I was wise to wait until the 50 line WAS crossed.

But somewhere along the line you have to draw a line in the sand and say, "These are my rules, and I won't break them". Usually it evens out. Sometimes you get the pips right off the bat, and other times you don't. But changing rules every other trade will ultimately be disastrous.

That being said, there is no reason you CAN'T put a 45/55 channel on the QQE and use it. Try it and see how it works for you. The main thing to consider is your 'comfort zone' or 'confidence zone' so to speak about entering AND exiting a trade. If that 45/55 channel helps you then by all means go for it 100%!  The QQE basically gives the same info as the RSI.  The ONLY reason I prefer the QQE is the audible alarm on the 50 crossing which is not available on the RSI.

Hi Jim,

I can't post my PDF file on the HAS candles. For some reason it's corrupted. But I'm sure there's someone lurking around here that has a copy of it. I see it frequently mentioned. The PDF file just gives a brief discussion on em, but you really learn so much more when you start watching them. Sorry I couldn't be more help. Meanwhile, while you're waiting, load up the HAS on different pairs, then go back and take a look at the HAS Candles on different time frames, paying attention to the wicks, their size and direction, particularly when you have a major trend change. You'll see frequently the 'major information HAS' on a highly probably trend change will be a small colored body with a different colored wick. That's about the best synopsis or help I can offer right now.

Re: Losing pips. Gotta tell you in all honesty . . . nothin' I have going right now is working well. Market's are crazy! Just about the time I see my indicators line up - BAM - it goes haywire. I'm only posting this because (while it's true that many systems stop working after awhile for various reasons) don't be too quick to abandon whatever system/strategy/method and indicators you've grown to like and use recently. New President - new economic recovery package in the works - global economic melt-downs - usual bad time of year to trade - has all contributed to the forex being unpredictable.

This is just a really bad time period to say 'it's business as usual'. But it WILL improve - maybe not the economy here so quickly, but the forex WILL settle down again.

3°) or  CCI89 is still (<0) & cci 21 who was >0 becomes now <0 on crossing zeroline  accordind with others indies you can SHORT

Hello every body

I have been following this system since Canadian with some good results. But from two weeks ago I am filtering the trades with the Double CCI in 5min and taking signals and trades in 1min, and it looks to be working. I put some chars for explaining better.

This is in 5 min TF:I look for buy signals if both the 24 and 79 ccis are over (or      touching in going up) the 30 sma line and 0 line, it does not matter which      one get over first. I look for sell signal if both the 24 and 79 are under (or      touching in going down) the 30 sma line and 0 line , it does not matter which      one get down first. It finish when the 24 cci takes again the sma30.

Orange vertical lines are the trades in 1 min..

Hope it helps.

Sorry for my poor English.

Best regards

--- 帖子 #1391 ---
The Read me text:

I. Features:

This is an improved version of period converter for MT4 based on the

MT4's default period converter by metaquotes.

The default period converter script do not support real-time refreshing,

and consume lots of CPU (50%-9x%) making the whole system slow.

Also, the default one is a script which do not save when you exit MT4,

so you have to apply every converter script again after restarting, quite

annoying.

This one fixed all above problems:

1. Real-time updating or custom interval millisecond level updating.

2. Low CPU cost, average 5%-10% or less.

3. Works as an indicator, so can be saved and reloaded during restart.

4. There is no one converter per chart limitation as it is not script

any more, you can only use one window as source to generate as many

new timeframe chart as possible.

5. Auto updating if there is new history block loaded.

II. How to use:

Copy the mq4 file to your MT4 indicators folder (expertsindicators)

to install it as an indicator, NOT script. then in the custom indicator

list, attach period_converter_opt to the chart you want.

It support 4 parameters:

PeriodMultiplier: new period multiplier factor, default is 2

UpdateInterval: update interval in milliseconds,

zero means update real-time. default is zero.

Enabled: You can disable it without remove it with this option.

Other parameters are comments or for debugging, it is safe to ignore them.

Also Make sure you have Allow Dll imports option checked in common tab or

it won't work

After that, File->Open Offline to open the generated offline data. then

the offline data will be updated automatically.

As long as you keep the source chart open and the converter indicator

running, the generated chart including indicators inside will always

be updated. also you can close the generated chart and open again

later from File->Open Offline without problem.

If you want to quit MT4, you can leave those offline chart as other

normal online charts. when you start MT4 next time, those charts will

also be loaded and updated.

III. Notes:

1. Do NOT uncheck the "offline chart" option in offline chart common properties.

or after MT4 restart, it will treat that chart as online chart and request

the data from server, resulting empty chart window.

2. You can attach more than one converter to same window with different

PeriodMultiplier, e.g: you can attach 3 converter with

PeriodMultiplier = 2, 4, 10 to M1 to generate M2, M4, M10 at the same time.

It is even ok to use the M1 chart to generate Hourly chart like H2, which

only cost a few more CPU resource during initial conversion. but usually

most server don't have much data for those short period. resulting the

generated data isn't long enough for long period. so it is suggested

to use Hourly/Daily charts as source when needed.

3. The real-time updating mode updates quotes as fast as possible, but as

this is done via script, and MT will skip calling start() function when

your PC is busy and lots of quotes income. anyway, this seldom happen,

and you can at least get 10 updates each seconds which is much more

than enough.

4. The offline chart don't have a bid line showing in chart, but all data

in the chart including the indicators is still being updated,

so don't worry. you can show the bid line by unclick the "offline chart"

option in chart properties. but which don't helps much and if you forget

to check "offline chart" option before exit. it will cause errors and

become empty on next startup. you have to close the window and open

again from File->Open offline, which don't worth the trouble.

IV. History:

2005.12.24 1.4 faster to detect if data changed by removing float point

operations, added support to output CSV file in real time.

OutputCSVFile = 0 means no CSV.

OutputCSVFile = 1 means CSV + HST

OutputCSVFile = 2 CSV only, no HST .

(useful if you want to generate CSV for builtin periods)

CSV Filename will be the same as HST file except the extension.

added safe checking for PeriodMultiplier.

2005.12.04 1.3 Fixed missing data when there is large amount of data

loaded in several blocks, and support auto updating

when new history is loaded.

2005.11.29 1.2 Additional fix for missing data and server changing.

2005.11.29 1.1 Fixed missing partial data after restart.

Reinitialize after changing server or data corrupted.

2005.11.28 1.0 Initial release.

Just don't close the 1 min chart once you have the 2 min chart working.

[quote=kinonen;2528555]
Hi Kino,

I don't want to come across like Mr Know-it-all and certainly don't want to kick in open doors, but since you have not traded a live account yet..... I want to give you a bit of advice, for I know that most traders have experienced a big difference trading demo versus real live account..... which has to do with emotion and fear of loosing real money.

There are a few things to consider before starting a live account. Maybe you have done this already and am I writing this invain..... In that case someone else may consider these matters:

1. Take care that you have a good (MM) money management system. You can't do without it.

2. If you are scalping like the FX-50 system it is very useful to place and close your orders using 1 or 2 Click scripts. For in real live scalping it's sometimes a matter of seconds between a "winner" or a "looser".

Quite often some brokers requote prices when you want to open a trade. A script will take of that immediately.

Some scripts for taking longs and shorts have already a built-in MM-decision, which eases taking postions.

3. Consider starting with an account of no more than 2000 and build it up. I know it's tempting to start with a bigger account, for everyone always imagines great wins..... but your losses at the beginning will also be bigger.

Many years ago I had to learn it the hard way.....

Cheers, John

[quote=Dan Johnston;2529903]
Hi Dan,

Last year...... and more often since the start of the global financial crises some brokers nowadays more and more start behaving like ordinary thieves..... just stealing more and more pips right at the moment you want to open a trade.

One phenomenon in this respect is the all of a sudden widening of spread at irregular intervals. For instance EURGBP is targeted with several brokers quite recently with pipspreads as wide from 3 to 20 at around 20 GMT upto 04 GMT. So be careful and check with your broker what they are up to tomorrow..... next week..... or in the near future.....

They also do that with the fixed spread currency pairs like EURUSD by all of a sudden popping up "Requote" screens. It' s obvious they want to disorientate you right at that moment and have you click away on that pop up.

In the beginning I have done that as well and noticed sometimes pipspread losses on EurUSD for as much as 8 pips instead of the usual 2.

Here are some scripts..... You may have to try them and see which ones work with your broker, for I have noticed difference of function of these scripts between brokers as well.

To adjust MM decision and the like just open these scripts in Metaeditor and fill in your personal needs regarding TP and SL.

Before using those scripts...... do test them on a demo account with the same broker you have your live account !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!

Good Luck, John

--- 帖子 #1453 ---
On the screen you see T3MA 36/0.59 (Red= Ribbon and Magenta=Single) and T3MA 54/0.63 (Green=Ribbon and Lime=Single). Only the T3MA Single (Magenta and Lime) versions show the right curves.

What I have noticed is that on the T3MA Ribbon you can't change the VolumeFactor...... any figure below 0.99 in reality presents 0.7 for Volme Factor on the Ribbon version. Using a figure of 1 and higher only wil give a different VolumeFactor influence on this indicator.

So what you see here on the Ribbon version is always a VolumeFactor of 0.7 no matter what you would fill in here below 1.0 .....

B.T.W. There is another issue regarding refreshing....

I know it's a lagging indicator..... but I promise you absolutely will be surprised for what purpose it will be used. When finshed I will give a full explanation in detail......

--- 帖子 #1456 ---
Hi Kino,

The T3MA is specially designed for using Volume Factors below 1..... so in the range of 0.13 upto 0.99.

Actually you normally wouldn't use any Volume Factor above the value of 1.

When you substitute different numbers in that range you should notice highs and lows expand with higher values out of that range..... say for instance a value of 0.81....

Subsequently you should see a decrease of highs and lows when using values on the lower side of that range.... say for instance 0.27.....

You can check how this should function..... using the single T3MA version first and next compare how this should funtion in the same way with the ribbon version.

Now when you substitute in the current Ribbon Version any value between 0.13 and 0.99 into the Volume factor fields you will notice nothing will happen to the highs and lows, i.e. it will in all cases present the same curve ..... as if in all cases 0.7 would have been substituted for value.....

I hope you do understand me now?

Regards, John
