--- 帖子 #2222 ---
Hi Pipster,

I follow your reasoning, however you made a major mistake. If you look at both setups on this chart...... you know immediately why..... Your retracement didn't happen above or under all Zones..... instead it happened inside quite a narrow TF30 Zone.

It should be like it's the case at the end of this chart. Nevertheless there is much hesitation here as well because of all the Spudfibo's overhead. Please check the chart below.

A retracement is only to be considered powerful and valid....... in open space..... whenever that retracement of TF1Zone occurs towards TF5Zone (and in some cases towards TF15Zone).

When between TFZones the same has to be true..... there also has to be enough open space when between TFZones..... for price to be able to jump out of TF1Zone (longs) or to fall out of TF1Zone (shorts).

Open space = when Pipdistance towards another TFZone or Fib- or Pivotline is more than 35 Pips.

So watch it and good luck next time, John

--- 帖子 #2251 ---
Hi John,

This indi is based on Zigzag indicator and there is no reference point for it such as daily open or daily high or fixed hours...

I mean it just draws  fibo levels between 2 points of zigzag peaks , it will change everytime zigzag peak changes (the highest and lowest peaks in a special range which could be defined). I think  if you change the color (in the color tab from 255,255,255 to another one) you'll understand what I mean...

As you know the zigzag is an amazing indicator which pointing to the short trends and price retracements, but you should know how to set the settings for every timeframes to eliminate the noise. You can also change the ExtDepth value (for the mentioned special range) to find out what settings work best for your time frame.

Reza

--- 帖子 #2262 ---
hi ;  new version 2 (before 3 , 4 etc ...) so How that works =

with a simple glance if you see that  ALL the nb of pips to close are red = then close is below all ribbons , green above cool no ?

nb pips to close is red = close is below this ribbon , green above
CCIs are red or green (below or above a level you can change = zero , 100; -67 or +67 or 228 lol) and you can change also periods of CCIs
RSI 8 is red below or above a level that you can change =45, 55 or 50 or 80) and you also can change also period of RSI
Price is Green if up and Red if down
ADX is Green if > 20 or else and Red if <0
SMA 50 or else is red if above bar close , Green below
Time to next bar nothing to precise
local time   nothing to precise !

if you want something else let me know !

kino

Hi Satini,

I hope you don't mind if I take a minute to answer your question, I saw your post was 25 hours old. John can complement if he can give further insights.

The second entry was a very good High Probability Trade setup. Price bounced up from closing TF5 zone together with TF1 which indicates strong support. No TF zones ahead which you can easely see on both Kino indicators. CCI has strong momentum, and both FX primes pointing to uptrend.

Your entry on the first arrow was not a high prob trade. Congrats with the pips, I think you made a nice ride. However, it wasn't a safe entry. Close above you, in the direction of your trade, you have got resistance from TF5 zone, which didn't gave support short before. TF 5 zone was just trying to turn to a closing triangle. At your entry point it was not clear that TF1 zone was giving this support and was able to win over TF5 resistance.

CCI had negative momentum! The longer FXPrime indicator was neutral and didn't paint the white alert dots.

Waiting for TF1 zone retracing to TF5 was a possibility. It doens't happen all the time. CCI indicated good health (no divergence) so it was good to enter here.

--- 帖子 #2280 ---
Welcome Mike!

The best thing you can do is learning the stuff from the pdf and get familiair with the template from post#1.

In this thread you can also find the newest developments like the indicator on which you're questioning about. It's a really good one, I like it.

In this indicator there are several components which don't really belong to this Ribbon system.

When something new is tested and can fit into the system, it will be in the next update in post#1. So you can wait to learn all indicators which are (and will be) posted.

But if you wat to know the MonitorV2: Take a look at my picture.

The ADX ad RSI values aren't part of our system. SMA50 isn't also.

CCI21 isn't used in the latest templates anymore. This CCi21 is integrated in the upper FXPrime indicator. But to show you what it is, I placed a doubleCCi in my chart below. You can forget about it. Or remember: if it's green and positive, the entryCCi is above zero (and vice versa).

If the distances from the ribbons are all red, that means price is below all ribbons (look for short high probability trades).

If the distances from the ribbons are all green, that means price is below all ribbons (look for long high probability trades).

Maybe you want to trade between the ribbons (that's where distances are red AND green). You can now easely look if pipdistance is >35 pips, which is a requirement.

Hope this helps you.

Cheers, Jazz

--- 帖子 #2318 ---
First of all: my excuses for my previous post!

I hoped I could find time this week for trading and posting on this thread, but it's different.

Okay, I want to show you 2 pics.

Reason is the orchid coloured TF30 Zone. I think it is good to repeat what John told about that Zone at the time he introduced it. He said:

"You will notice that TF30Zone is of less importance for entry decision and actually is more or less only usefull to identify support and resistance at greater distances. As such the edges of TF30Zone (=TF30Ribbon) most of the time work more the same as Pivot-and Fiblines."

That's my opinion on the TF30 Zone too. Actually I have to say that if you don't pay attention to that principle, you will mis the boat and (even worse) will entry too late /getting in bad trades.

However the TF30 Zone is on my charts for reason the 'pivot' function.

NB: Because of the original intention of the TF30 Zone, the #Kino_close_above_ribbons indicator doesn't have TF30 Zone in it's calculation.

pay attention to the big distance between Yesterdays High which is reached on the chart and yellow TF5 zone. In my opinion it happens often that price retraces to this Zone. In this case it was much further.

For those who think: Jazz' chart is different from mine......yes, I had data probems....I am missing half an hour data.

Hello all,

Btw just my opinion, may be others can correct me out. Based on Figure 1 ( Zoom In version), it does seems that price is continuing an uptrend, and the blue ribbon below seems to show that there is a support for it.

But sometimes it is good also to zoom out a little and see how others ribbon is doing. Figure 2 is the zoom out version of the same trade.

1. Here you can see that TF5 is going to clash with TF15. Probably not a good time to trade because we do not know which one will win, TF5 or TF15, and where will price go after the clash? Also if you look closer at the TF5 ribbon, it is widening so less support to push price up.

2. Blue ribbon is also not widening or narrowing. If narrowing, we could at least assume TF15 is supporting uptrend. Or if blue ribbon is widening, we could assume that price will go down through it.

3. Pink ribbon is widening, so this also show that there is no support from all ribbon to push the price up.

So as you can see, price go down after that. A short would have been really nice. Anyway thats what I understand from reading the thread, hope others can correct my mistakes. Thanks.

--- 帖子 #2338 ---
It's a game between the next factors. Talking about an upmove:

- is CCI strong? Negative Divergence into CCI has to make you careful.

- is the support from TF zones strong? e.g. if TF5 zone is far below, it's risky because these traders can take profit near an important pivot or fibo level. But if two or more TF edges are very nearby, then they can give strong support.

- did price already made a strong upmove? If yes, be carefull.

See my attachment. Price breaks out all Zones and comes near to Yesterdays High Pivot. Then it falls back to exactly TF1 Zone and goes up again. Take a sharp look at CCI, which doesn't come high again, showing negative divergence. This is a warning that the pivot can be too strong. Pipdistance to  Y-High is very small and Y-High is an important pivot. So if you made your entry on the first vertical line, you better be extra carefull.

Price falls down, making lower lows an a lower high. New down move? I don't think so! Much support overhere from TF5 and TF15 and TF30.

Now I am going to wait for CCI breaking the yellow resistance trendline. If that occurs I can try a long. It happened...I made my entry long, and.....my internet connection and telephone broke down....WOW....okay, call my broker by cell phone and closed my position with a little profit above the pivot!

Your question about pipdistance.... I think 15 pips at minimum. John, what's your opinion? I am not trading Forex, I think most people know that overhere. I am trading FESX index. This system also works on Indexes, futures etcetera.

The trade I made here was too close to the pivotline, but I wanted to beat it. Usually I take around a wave length as minimum. But that's no rule.

I don't think you could have known about the upcoming clash, it's in the future. If price would have made a strong upmove, the clash didn't happen!

The point is, the blue and pink zones are quiet at distance. Instead of thinking they will give support, I think they first have a certain attraction on price, like a magnet. A breakout is much stronger if most or all of teh zones are just below price.

Yes, if pipdistance >35 pips, trading between the ribbons is a good possibility.

--- 帖子 #2415 ---
I have been using the JE Ribbon system and have found it very good. I would like to share what I have found to be the real power in the system. I found using the TF1 ribbon allows you to be caught up too much in the whipsaw effect. I have found the real power to be in the TF5 ribbon. To be more precise - when the Tick Ribbon moves above and below the TF5 Ribbon. (I have found it easier to just have a 13 ema instead of the Tick Ribbon). Trading these ribbons provides very good risk/reward ratios most of the time and lets you cut your losses short and your profits run. I also use the double cci with sma with settings of 480 for the trend cci and 200 for the sma - this provides a very good filter for removing the crosses that dont go anywhere. S&R levels are important for exits along with Fib Extentions. It is the best system I have used and has produced consistent good profits. Below is an example of how it even works in a relatively flat market.

http://i5.photobucket.com/albums/y16...vot_210709.jpg

--- 帖子 #2419 ---
For longs - when the 13 ema has moved through the top of the TF5 ribbon and the cci is green or has just crossed above the zero line.

For shorts - when the 13 ema has moved through the bottom of the TF5 ribbon and the cci is orange or has just crossed below the zero line.

The sma also gives a clue as to direction and the other higher TF ribbons along with fib and Murrey Math S&R levels give further evidence of how good the trade is and when to exit.

I am not interested in trading the short term chop, I want high probable trades and the 480 cci gives me that and works well with the 13ema/TF5 crosses.

--- 帖子 #2428 ---
The easiest exit is when the 13ema crosses back into the TF5 Ribbon. However that is mostly a late exit and you will have given up profits. I use Elliott wave with Fib retracements and extentions. I look for clusters, ie,. on extentions after retracements I look for support or resistance levels and a murrey math level that fall on the extentions of 127%, 138%, 161% or even 261%. If there is a clear cluster then I will set my limit there. On retracement (counter trend) trades (which have to have a clear risk/reward of more than 2 to 1) I look for a cluster around the fib levels 38.2%, 50% or 61.8%.

I believe in the rule of not letting a winner turn into a loser. So I pull my stop up to break even when about 20 pips up and move it up under obvious pull backs. It is a juggling act of protecting your profits and still giving the trade room. Another method would be to keep moving your stop to just the other side of the TF5 ribbon.

You could also use the Smoothed Heikenashi candles as per FX-prime for your exits, but I also find them to give a late exit.

I am happy to hear any better suggestions.

I trade this system live on the Eur/Usd.

--- 帖子 #2429 ---
In case some are trying/using this system with my template, I have made an adjustment to the CCI/SMA settings - change the entry cci number to 300. This gives a better sma tradjectory.

Long entries - the cci must be above zero and above the sma and you must wait for the sma to also be above zero.

Short entries - opposite of above.

I have found this to filter out a lot of the trades that go nowhere. You must also pay attention to the higher TF ribbons as per J.E.'s recommendations.

I recommend the use of the simulator posted back on page 92 of this thread. It is a great way to not only test a system, but also to cram a lot of learning and get to know a system.

I run it at full speed and when a signal is given, knock it back to normal speed, place the order, then crank it up again. Run it while the market is slow and you are waiting for a setup.

I have found it very helpful in getting to know when and when not to take a signal based on what the higher TF ribbons are doing.

--- 帖子 #2439 ---
After some more intensive testing I believe I have improved the system even further. I have found it to be so, but you will have to test it and make your own judgement. In case anyone would like to test/use it I have attached it.

The cci is gone as the moving averages in the ribbons tell the same thing, so why have a double up of information. I have used sma's for the ribbons as I could get them to reflect price movement more accurately.

Fxprime is there just for extra confirmation.

The 2MA Crossover arrows are not an entry signal. They are just an early warning that an entry may be about to happen. This is so you dont have to sit there and watch the computer all the time.

Entry: When the 13ema crosses through the TF5 ribbon and fxprime says go and you have no obstruction from the higher TF ribbons.

Exit: When the 13ema crosses back right through the TF5 ribbon or when a fibretracement/fibextention is hit.

Stop loss: 5 pips or so under or above the TF5 ribbon (depending on long or short entry). If your risk level allows it, to give extra room place it under/above the previous swing high/low.

Happy Pipping!

Hello Wakayama I'm in the same situation than you but maybe this can help.

1) I saw that in some cases before the "second high probability trade" appear a white dot in the fxprime v2 alerting the proximation of the trade (like you can see in your example).

2) Look at kijuntenkan to be aligned with 1M kino or going down 1M kino

(I think this is important)

3) Wait for the 5M kino to be wide and take trend.

4) wait for retracement of TrandCCi

If you take this as rule, you dont enter in trade 1 because rule 1,2,3 and 4

In trade 2 I spect price going down for elliot wave, not going up, anyway you can see trendCCi down and 5Mkino taking trend down.

In trade 3 you can see all 4 "rules" completed, an elliot wave move, TrendCCi strongth enought and CCi SMA crossing 0.

I hope this can help you.

Luis

--- 帖子 #2499 ---
No problem.

I have them grouped as they relate to one another.

EURUSD, USDJPY, EURJPY. (The eurjpy movement is the eurusd x usdjpy.)

GBPUSD, GPBJPY, EURGBP. (The gbpjpy movement is the gbpusd x usdjpy)

AUDUSD, AUDJPY, EURAUD. (The audjpy movement is the aususd x usdjpy)

USDCAD

USDCHF

NZDUSD

If you do some research on Correlation you will get an idea of which move in relation to one another. For example the EURUSD and USDCHF mostly mirror each other, and the Commodity Currencies, AUDUSD, USDCAD, NZDUSD all tend to move similarly.

By watching so many pairs it gives you a better idea of movements and you can pick the best signal out of them for the best risk/reward.

cheers.

--- 帖子 #2514 ---
Being in Australia I trade the Asian and half the London sessions. There are at least 3 good signals a day in these sessions. I quite often wake up to see really good signals and movement in the New York session particularly on the EURUSD. I only take one signal/trade at a time, but the reason I watch so many pairs is that it gives you a choice between the correlated pairs to pick the signal with the best position (risk/reward).

The system so far this month has shown a 72% success rate, and netted a 14% increase in my account. This could have been a more if I had of let more trades run. I am now seeing that using an M1 chart and a H1 chart together on the same pair improves targets and trade lengths.

If there is enough interest I may think about starting a new trading thread for this system where we can focus on it and use it to greater success.

--- 帖子 #2557 ---
Hi,

I am not really interested in other teading systems. Each trading system is really like having a business. Best to focus on one. Each has it ups and downs.

Best to stick to one and really get to know it then to jump around from method to method.

Good trading system:

1) + expectancy

2) Low risk

3) Wins over the long term

4) Completely automatic and automated. This is a huge factor for me. I'd rather make 20% on auto pilto then 30% bu have to watch the markets all day.

The biggest problem most new traders face is they are bombarded with get rich quick....Lower your expectancy and decide if trading is for you or not. This isn't a hobby.

--- 帖子 #2575 ---
Hi There,

In order to import more 1 minute bars you can do the following:

- press and hold 'Home' key (fn+left arrow on Mac) on desired 1 min chart until the chart stops

scrolling. It will download more bars from the server. The fastest way doing it is to zoom out

maximally the 1 min chart first and then press the 'Home' key.

- alternatively you can go to the history center (press F2), select desired symbol's 1 minhistory and press the 'Downlad' button.

Hope this helps

P07

--- 帖子 #2626 ---
I just wanted to attach a chart to show the power of what Kino has done with the ICHI. This is a Bare 15 minute chart with no indicators. The Senkou Span B is the flatter thicker part of the Kumo Cloud. Just like with the RIBBONS you can see how resistance and support can work off of each time period Kumo and Senkou  Span B. I also attached an excellent pdf on the ICHI by some pros who trade this style. I will also attach my template which emphasizes those areas that are important to understand by there thickness. You will see on the chart I posted how price once clear the 15 Minute  Senkou Span B than finds resistance at the 30 minute and 60 minute Senkou Span B before breaking free for a short long. You can also see nicely how the Senkou Span B than switches to become the flat base of each Kumo cloud on all the time frames. If you look to the dark brown area of the right bottom corner of the  template you can see that on the 4 hour kumo the SenKou Span B would already have to be support because all you can see is Senkou Span A. This is another really GREAT contribution Kino has made to this thread taking what he has learned and applying it to the ICHI. It also is in line of John's very visual way of trading the RIBBONS. It also works just fine with the FX indicator system settings for the CCI. The power of the ICHI is it can be a whole system without indicators at the bottom of the chart. The ICHI was designed so you could trade with out indicators. I have always liked the ICHI but this MTF view of it is extremely powerful and what I have been looking for to trade it.

--- 帖子 #2632 ---
This chart looks congested at first but watch how there is a high probability cross of the green TENKAN SEN above the white KIJUN SEN at the yellow arrow. It than rises through the gray 30 minute time zone spans A and B but takes its time. It hesitates at the red Senkou Span A (dashes) of the 240 minute. It crosses after some hour hesitation at the 60 minute green thick Senkou Span A. It than jumps to the red thick Senkou Span A of the 240 minute time zone. After several hours it breaks through until price finally exhaust itself. It than is falling back to the base 15 minute time zone of the chart where it starting to catch support from the aqua A Senkou Span.

At the same time you will see on the chart each time zone Ichimoku do the a Senkou Span Twist with resistance becoming support. Looking at a chart with the Kino Ichimoku tool is fascinating. Seeing support like this can help you stick with a trade longer than you might if you were looking a chart with out the Kino Ichimoku tool. .

--- 帖子 #2633 ---
This is not a trade but here is a ranging EURCHF chart right before FOMC today. I was wondering what the influence of the 1440 time period or Daily Senkou Spans would be on a chart as small as  the 15 minute chart period. The purple line is the Senkou Span A of the 1440 as it runs through the 15 minute and 30 minute clouds. I just put the spans of these large time periods because their clouds are often so big you are trading inside them or outside them. I do the same thing with the 240 minute. Multiple times price comes down and touches the purple span and at the end is consolidating around the span. Every higher time period span can impact the 15 minute chart. So to some up. The chart is based on the 15 minute period with the Ichimoku of this period the primary trading system. The higher time period Ichimoku clouds and their spans can be seen on the chart except for the 240 minute or 4 hour and 1440 minute or Daily. With these I just place the spans not to clutter the chart. They are there to see resistance and support. It would seem that the Kino MTF ICHIMOKU displays dynamically support and resistance. The trend CCI is there with the -67 to 67 area blacked out as a filter. I also use a multi-time period RSI as a filter on my chart. All ideas from this thread. There is an ATR superimposed over the CCI as a volatility or enthusiasm indicator often getting an increase in ATR prior to a big move. I use tick volume on my charts and find it useful.

Hey samanfx,

the thread you are in right now is a good on.

The other one I can refer you to is this one: http://www.forexfactory.com/showthread.php?t=490220

--- 帖子 #2675 ---
Hello,

the guy that started the original threat turned out to be a scammer. In the end he wanted to sell his indicator's and his Setup.

The original System is based on a 170 CCI, a 34 CCI and a RSI between Level 45 and 55.

If 170 and 34 are above 0 and RSI is above Level 55, then you buy and sell if the reverse is the case. This System is good and easy to follow. The next question you have to ask yourself is: What timeframe do you want to trade in?

Let me know.

D.
